- Source of truth is TrinityCore C++ 3.4.3 build 12340/TDB442 in `/home/server/woltk-trinity-legacy`.
- Do not use Retail, Cataclysm, 3.3.5, C#, or CypherCore as authority.

- Commit locally only after independent review plus validation.

## Progress Estimate

Overall core migration estimate with #522 represented `SendGameObjectDespawn` shared-vision target in-world gate remains conservatively `~94.5%` (do not claim >95% until ownership/runtime gaps below are substantially closed). #522 closes only the bounded session-side guard that canonical typed Player/Creature shared-vision targets must still be `in_world` before acting as represented `viewer->m_seer == target` fanout targets for `SMSG_GAMEOBJECT_DESPAWN`; it does not add a new runtime/manual-test milestone. The latest #505-#522 work lets logged-in `WorldSession::process_pending()` consume map-owned GameObject/DynamicObject update evidence through represented session packets under increasingly C++-anchored receiver gates, without claiming full runtime/global fanout.

This remains intentionally below the R8 TSV row-completion ratio because heavy runtime ownership gaps remain. ObjectAccessor has typed map-local read seams over canonical `MapObjectRecord` for several families plus a limited typed Player global-registry seam, `Map::RemoveAllObjectsInRemoveList` represents switch-list and deferred remove-list drains, supported Creature/GameObject loaded-grid respawn inputs have bounded map-owned seams, and `ManagedMap::update` now consumes #449 represented DynamicMapTree head update before instrumentation/later phases, represented DynamicObject, AreaTrigger, Creature, Conversation, SceneObject, GameObject, #439 Transport visitation, #440 MultiPersonalPhaseTracker expiry helpers, #442 live Creature/GameObject/AreaTrigger move-list drains, #443 represented `ProcessRelocationNotifies` source gating/marked-cell consumption, and #444 represented `DelayedUnitRelocation` visibility/AI plan exposure before reset, plus #445 represented `SendObjectUpdates` update-flag/mask consumption, #446 represented script-schedule processing, #447 represented map-owned weather timer/default-weather update/reset before personal phase, #448 represented tail ScriptMgr/metrics boundary, #450 represented DynamicMapTree insert/remove/contains model-key facade, #451 exact GameObject add/remove consumption of explicit model evidence, #452 represented `CreateModel()` map-object flag plus `EnableCollision(toggledState)` evidence, #453 represented `GameObject::UpdateModel()` model-key refresh over canonical exact typed GameObject records, #454 locally represents the map-owned `GameObject::SetDisplayId -> UpdateModel` caller order seam, #455 locally represents `GameObject::SetGoState -> EnableCollision` caller order/evidence, #456 adds the represented map-owned `SetLootState` collision/restock caller seam, #457 consumes it from represented loot release, #458-#460 consume linked-trap/ClearLoot/GOOBER pre-branch ordering inside `GameObject::Update`, #461 adds the bounded non-consumed chest/goober post-`ClearLoot()` early return. These are still narrow represented/runtime-dependency slices, not full live parity: ObjectAccessor/live AddToWorld/fanout/scripts/visibility, several runtime loaders, creature vehicle templates, GameObject AI/go-type/per-player/loot/model/collision/visibility/transport behavior, Transport AI/scripts/spline/teleport/passenger/static-passenger/fanout runtime, exact TypeContainerVisitor/order/cell traversal, real terrain/vmap/dynamic-tree collision/BIH/LOS/intersections/heights, real GameObjectModel geometry/model-store hydration, Transport delayed-add model runtime, live `SetDisplayId()`/`SetGoState()` caller consumption outside these facades, DB save/delete execution for runtime branches, full relocation notifier side effects/visibility/fanout/runtime, full personal-phase visibility/fanout/runtime, real script command execution/script manager hooks/destruction count integration, real WeatherMgr/weather regeneration/player-count/fanout/script-hook runtime, and broader Unit/Player inventory/auras/threat/motion/update-field work remain open.

## Remaining Gaps / Next Dependency

`#NEXT.R8.ENTITIES.405` corrects only the DB-backed data/builder dependency for the pure Creature loaded-grid resolver/loader closure; it does **not** complete full live respawn/runtime ownership. Remaining heavy dependencies toward >95% core include:

1. Wire the now-available DB-backed Creature loader inputs into the live world-server loaded-grid `DoRespawn` closure: select the map-owned runtime GUID from the `&mut Map` seam, compose `CreatureLoadedGridLifecycleResolverLikeCpp`, and pass typed `MapObjectRecord::Creature` records into `Map::process_due_respawns_composite_loaded_grid_respawns_like_cpp` without holding map locks across DB/async work.
2. Complete creature vehicle-template runtime beyond #465's represented identity/local-kit seam before treating those spawns as full runtime complete; real VehicleKit seat data/install/uninstall, AddToWorld, ZoneScript, AI, ObjectAccessor/fanout, dynamic tree/collision, packets and DB persistence remain open.
3. Add the equivalent GameObject DB-backed loader bridge/wiring into the same loaded-grid `DoRespawn` seam, preserving #398 lifecycle validation and no fake transport/template fallbacks.
4. Execute real live `PoolMgr` Spawn1Object/ReSpawn1Object/Despawn1Object from the existing action records, including loaded-grid loader invocation, DB respawn save/delete ownership, recursive subpool execution, and deterministic/true RNG integration where required.
5. Complete `AddToWorld`/`RemoveFromWorld`, ObjectAccessor map-local ownership, grid/session fanout, dynamic tree/collision hooks, scripts/AI/vehicle/zonescript initialization, and cleanup side effects after typed records enter/leave `Map`.
6. Continue reducing Player/Unit/Creature/GameObject lifecycle, UpdateFields, inventory/equipment, auras, threat, motion, spawn/despawn/respawn and AreaTrigger runtime gaps.

Recommended next slice after #465: choose the next heavy runtime dependency rather than adding cosmetic helpers. Highest-value options are loaded-grid GameObject DB-backed `Create/LoadFromDB` wiring into the same `&mut Map` respawn seam, or Creature/Vehicle runtime after the represented vehicle-template identity/local-kit seam; both require fresh C++ anchors and honest scoped acceptance, and neither may fake missing AddToWorld/ObjectAccessor/fanout/scripts/AI/zonescript/formation/dynamic-tree side effects as complete.
